Player Passing 2026 Major League Soccer Table

### About FBref.com

FBref.com launched (June 13, 2018) with domestic league coverage for England, France, Germany, Italy, Spain, and United States. Since then we have been steadily expanding our coverage to include domestic leagues from over 40 countries as well as domestic cup, super cup and youth leagues from top European countries. We have also added coverage for major international cups such as the [UEFA Champions League](https://fbref.com/en/comps/8/UEFA-Champions-League-Stats) and [Copa Libertadores](https://fbref.com/en/comps/14/Copa-Libertadores-Stats).


FBref is the most complete sources for women's football data on the internet. This includes the entire history of the [FIFA Women's World Cup](https://fbref.com/en/comps/106/history/Womens-World-Cup-Seasons) as well as recent domestic league seasons from nine countries.


View Additional Information

Note that player records are likely not complete for their careers. Players may come from or move to leagues we don't currently cover. This issue will go down over time, as we add new leagues and seasons.


You can sign up to [receive an e-mail](https://fbref.com/email) when new countries and features launch.

For more information, see our [Launch Blog Post](https://www.sports-reference.com/blog/2018/06/fbref-com-launches-today), the overall [leagues/competition page](https://fbref.com/en/comps) with details on leagues and seasons we include, or our [About Page](https://fbref.com/en/about//). [Let us know if you find an issue or have a suggestion](https://fbref.com/feedback/).

FBref is one of seven [Sports-Reference.com](https://www.sports-reference.com/) sites.
